#######################
# LUSTRIA Events
#######################
# lustria.0		# on_startup trigger event to set the jungles of lustria province modifiers
# lustria.1		# Manually add the modifier
# lustria.2		# on_five_year_pulse Lustrian jungle growth event (AI uses this event for clearing the jungles)
# lustria.3		# on_five_year_pulse Get sick due to the jungles of Lustria
# lustria.4		# Liege notified of courtier getting sick due to jungle
# lustria.5		# Liege notified of courtier dying due to sickness from jungle
# lustria.6		# on_decade_pulse Attacked by jungle beast
# lustria.7		# Creature challenges us to combat
# lustria.8		# Kill creature, no matter the outcome of the duel
# lustria.9		# on_decade_pulse Village disappears in the jungle
#######################
# lustria.10	# settlement_decision Choose whom you want to cut back your jungle
# lustria.11	# Event to resolve cutting back for the liege doing it himself
# lustria.12	# Tell character he has become sick due to cutting back the jungle
# lustria.13	# Character learns of his own success
# lustria.14	# Character learns of his own failure
# lustria.15	# Steward - Charged to cut back the Jungle
# lustria.16	# Liege is notified of success
# lustria.17	# Liege is notified of failure
#######################
# lustria.18	# on_five_year_pulse Spoils of the Lustrian jungle (lizardman only) grants random boon
# lustria.19	# Holy plaques found
# lustria.20	# Wild beasts tamed
# lustria.21	# Valuable resources found
#######################

namespace = lizardman
namespace = slizardmen
namespace = gslizard
namespace = lustria

#######################

# on_startup trigger event to set the jungles of lustria province modifiers
character_event = {
	id = lustria.0
	hide_window = yes

	only_rulers = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_save_game = no
		capital_scope = {
			location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			any_demesne_province = {
				limit = {
					location = {
						region = world_new_world_lustria 
						NOT={ duchy = { title = d_quetza } }
					}
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle }
				}
				# Manually add the modifier on startup
				province_event = {
					id = lustria.1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
# Manually add the modifier
province_event = {
	id = lustria.1
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = lustria_jungle
			duration = -1
		}
		# Set initial Modifier
		if = {
			limit = {
				holder_scope = {
					any_demesne_province = {
						location = { 
							region = world_new_world_lustria 
							NOT={ duchy = { title = d_quetza } }
						}
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle }
					}
				}
			}
			holder_scope = {
				any_demesne_province = {
					limit = {
						location = { 
							region = world_new_world_lustria 
							NOT={ duchy = { title = d_quetza } }
						}
						NOT = { has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle }
					}
					# Fire Event Recursively
					province_event = {
						id = lustria.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# Make it so the initial jungle level is random
		if = {
			limit = {
				location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
				NOR = {
					has_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
				}
			}
			# Make it so the initial jungle level is random
			random_list = {
				# Light Jungle
				25 = {
					# Kingdom level tier is more likely to have light jungle
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.0
						is_capital = yes
						holder_scope = {
							higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
						}
					}
					# Duke level is a bit more likely to have light jungle
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						is_capital = yes
						holder_scope = {
							real_tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					# Count level is a bit more likely to have light jungle
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						is_capital = yes
						holder_scope = {
							real_tier = COUNT
						}
					}
					# Ports and rivers more likely to have light jungle
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						OR = {
							borders_major_river = yes
							port = yes
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_light_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				# Medium Jungle
				25 = {
					# Ports and rivers more likely to have light jungle
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							borders_major_river = yes
							port = yes
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_medium_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				# Dense Jungle
				25 = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_dense_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				# Oppressive Jungle
				25 = {
					# Ports and rivers more likely to have light jungle
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							borders_major_river = yes
							port = yes
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_oppressive_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
# on_five_year_pulse Lustrian jungle growth event (AI uses this event for clearing the jungles)
character_event = {
	id = lustria.2
	desc = lizardman201desc
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_jungle"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_demesne_province = {
			location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
			terrain = jungle
			has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle }
				# AI manages its jungle with this event
				ROOT = {
					ai = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		# Jungle grows slower for natives
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			religion_group = old_ones_group
		}
		# Jungle grows slower in fuedal realms as they clear it
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.65
			is_tribal = no
			is_nomadic = no
		}
		# Jungle grows slower for tribal as they utilize the jungle more than their fuedal neighbors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			is_tribal = yes
		}
		# Jungle grows faster for nomads as they just pass through without affecting the jungle
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_nomadic = yes
		}
		# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.90
			realm_stewardship > 10
		}
		# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.80
			realm_stewardship > 15
		}
		# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.70
			realm_stewardship > 20
		}
		# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.60
			realm_stewardship > 25
		}
		# Jungle grows faster if more controlled
	}

	# Non AI Growth option
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			ai = no
		}
		any_demesne_province = {
			# Dense to Oppressive
			if = {
				limit = {
					location = { 
						region = world_new_world_lustria 
						terrain = jungle
						has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle
					}
					NOT={has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
					}
					remove_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_oppressive_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				# Medium to Dense
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
					}
					remove_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_dense_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				# Light to Medium
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
					}
					remove_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_medium_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
				# Light Jungle
				else = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_light_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# AI Growth Option
	option = {
		name = OK
		trigger = {
			ai = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			# Jungle Growth
			50 = {
				# More likely with low realm stewardship
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.2
					realm_stewardship < 15
				}
				any_demesne_province = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							location = { 
								region = world_new_world_lustria 
								terrain = jungle
								has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle
							}
							NOT={has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle}
						}
						# Dense to Oppressive
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
							}
							random_list={
								50 = {
									# Jungle grows slower next to rivers and coast (inland should be wilder and less useful)
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										OR = {
											borders_major_river = yes
											port = yes
										}
									}
									# Jungle grows slower next to rivers and coast (inland should be wilder and less useful)
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										any_neighbor_province = {
											OR = {
												borders_major_river = yes
												port = yes
											}
										}
									}
									# Jungle grows a little slower once it's dense
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
									}
									# Jungle grows slower next to fuedal realms as they clear it
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										any_neighbor_province = {
											is_tribal = no
											is_nomadic = no
										}
									}
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										ROOT = {
											is_tribal = no
											is_nomadic = no
										}
									}
									remove_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
									add_province_modifier = {
										name = lustria_oppressive_jungle
										duration = -1
									}
								}
								50 = {
								}
							}
						}
						# Medium to Dense
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
							}
							random_list={
								50 = {
									# Jungle grows slower next to rivers and coast (inland should be wilder and less useful)
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										OR = {
											borders_major_river = yes
											port = yes
										}
									}
									# Jungle grows slower next to rivers and coast (inland should be wilder and less useful)
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.8
										any_neighbor_province = {
											OR = {
												borders_major_river = yes
												port = yes
											}
										}
									}
									# Jungle grows slower next to fuedal realms as they clear it
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.9
										any_neighbor_province = {
											is_tribal = no
											is_nomadic = no
										}
									}
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.9
										ROOT = {
											is_tribal = no
											is_nomadic = no
										}
									}
									remove_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
									add_province_modifier = {
										name = lustria_dense_jungle
										duration = -1
									}
								}
								50 = {
								}
							}
						}
						# Light to Medium
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
							}
							random_list={
								50={
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.75
										has_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
									}
									# Jungle grows slower next to fuedal realms as they clear it
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.9
										any_neighbor_province = {
											is_tribal = no
											is_nomadic = no
										}
									}
									modifier = {
										factor = 0.9
										ROOT = {
											is_tribal = no
											is_nomadic = no
										}
									}
									remove_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
									add_province_modifier = {
										name = lustria_medium_jungle
										duration = -1
									}
								}
								50={
								
								}
							}
						}
						# Light Jungle
						else = {
							add_province_modifier = {
								name = lustria_light_jungle
								duration = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# Jungle CLearing
			50 = {
				# likely will not happen if the jungle is only Light
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					capital_scope = {
						has_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
					}
				}
				# Much less likely for the Lizardmen
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
					religion = old_ones
				}
				# Less likely for the Amazons/Pygmies
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					OR = {
						religion = amazon
						religion = kukaili
					}
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					realm_stewardship > 10
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					realm_stewardship > 15
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					realm_stewardship > 20
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					realm_stewardship > 25
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					independent = no
					top_liege = { realm_stewardship > 15 }
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					independent = no
					top_liege = { realm_stewardship > 20 }
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					independent = no
					top_liege = { realm_stewardship > 25 }
				}
				# Good realm stewardship keeps the jungle at bay
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					independent = no
					top_liege = { realm_stewardship > 30 }
				}
				any_demesne_province = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							location = { 
								region = world_new_world_lustria 
								terrain = jungle
								has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle
							}
						}
						# Oppressive to Dense
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
							}
							remove_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
							add_province_modifier = {
								name = lustria_dense_jungle
								duration = -1
							}
						}
						# Dense to Medium
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
							}
							remove_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
							add_province_modifier = {
								name = lustria_medium_jungle
								duration = -1
							}
						}
						# Medium to Light
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
							}
							remove_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
							add_province_modifier = {
								name = lustria_light_jungle
								duration = -1
							}
						}
						else = {
							random = {
								chance = 20
								remove_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# on_five_year_pulse Get sick due to the jungles of Lustria
character_event = {
	id = lustria.3
	desc = { 
		text = lizardman202courtierDesc
		trigger = { NOT = { event_target:target_character = { character = ROOT } } }
	}
	desc = { 
		text = lizardman202desc
		trigger = { event_target:target_character = { character = ROOT } }
	}
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_jungle"

	only_rulers = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#capital_scope = {
			location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle }
		#}
		NOT = { culture_group = lizardman_group }
	}
	immediate = {
		random_list={
			40={
				save_event_target_as = target_character 
			}
			40={
				trigger = {
					any_courtier = {
						location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
						location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle }
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = courtier_jungle_event
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
						location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle }
					}
					save_event_target_as = target_character 
				}
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		# Jungle Growth makes it more likely
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle }
		}
		# Jungle Growth makes it more likely
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.60
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle }
		}
		# Jungle Growth makes it more likely
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.35
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle }
		}
		# Low health makes it worse
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			health < 5
		}
		# Low health makes it worse
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			health < 10
		}
		# Existing illness gets worse
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			trait = ill
		}
		# Existing illness gets worse
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					trait = has_measles
					trait = has_typhus
					trait = has_tomb_rot
					trait = has_bone_auge
				 	trait = pneumonic
				 	trait = leper
					trait = syphilitic
				 	trait = pneumonic
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		# Without DLC Custom illness effect
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_dlc = "Reapers" }
			}
			random_list = {
				# Sickness
				85 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = { trait = ill }
						}
						random_list = {
							20 = {
								event_target:target_character = { 
									add_trait = has_measles
									nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
								}
							}
							20 = {
								event_target:target_character = { 
									add_trait = has_typhus 
									nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
								}
							}
							20 = {
								event_target:target_character = { 
									add_trait = has_tomb_rot
									nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
								}
							}
							20 = {
								event_target:target_character = { 
									add_trait = has_bone_auge 
									nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
								}
							}
							20 = {
								event_target:target_character = {
									add_trait = pneumonic 
									nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
								}
							}
						}
						# Notify liege
						if = {
							limit = {
								independent = no
								NOT={ event_target:target_character = { character = ROOT } }
							}
							liege = {
								# Liege notified of courtier getting sick due to jungle
								character_event = { id = lustria.4 }
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						event_target:target_character = { 
							add_trait = ill 
							nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
				# Death
				5 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:target_character = { trait = ill }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 5
						event_target:target_character = {
							OR = {
								trait = has_measles
								trait = has_typhus
								trait = has_tomb_rot
								trait = has_bone_auge
								trait = pneumonic
								trait = leper
								trait = syphilitic
								trait = pneumonic
							}
						}
					}
					# AntiDeath Effect
					if = {
						limit = { is_invincible_trigger = yes }
						antideath_effect = yes
						break = yes
					}
					# Notify liege
					if = {
						limit = {
							independent = no
							NOT={ event_target:target_character = { character = ROOT } }
						}
						liege = {
							# Liege notified of courtier dying due to sickness from jungle
							character_event = { id = lustria.5 }
						}
					}
					event_target:target_character = { death = { death_reason = death_trait } }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			event_target:target_character = { add_symptom_effect = yes }
		}
		clr_character_flag = courtier_jungle_event
	}
}
# Liege notified of courtier getting sick due to jungle
character_event = {
	id = lustria.4
	desc = lizardman203desc
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_jungle"
	notification = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

# on_decade_pulse Attacked by jungle beast
character_event = {
	id = lustria.6
	desc = { 
		text = lizardman205desc
		trigger = { NOT = { has_focus = focus_hunting } }
	
	}
	desc = { 
		text = lizardman205HuntDesc
		trigger = { has_focus = focus_hunting }
	
	}
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_dinosaur"

	only_rulers = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
		}
		OR = {
			in_command = yes
			trait = questing
			has_focus = focus_hunting
			has_character_flag = the_rush_of_hunt
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		# Jungle Growth makes it more likely
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle }
		}
		# Jungle Growth makes it more likely
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle }
		}
		# Jungle Growth makes it more likely
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		# Creature gets native name #Creatures: Razorbacks, Cold Ones, Terradons, Stegadon, Sauropod, Thunder Lizards, Carnosaur
		create_random_soldier = {
			random_traits = no
			dynasty = none
			religion = old_ones
			culture = lizardman
			name = " "
			female = no
			age = 30
			attributes = {
				martial = 5
				diplomacy = 0
				stewardship = 0
				learning = 0
				intrigue = 0
			}
		}
		# scope to character we created and make him send us a duel invite event - so we can't run away!
		new_character = {
			set_graphical_culture = generic_monster
			add_trait = creature_monster
			add_trait = wroth
			add_trait = brave
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_razorback
					change_martial = 5
					add_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
				}
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_cold_one
					change_martial = 6
					add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					if={
						limit={
							ROOT={ combat_rating >= 100 }
						}
						add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					}
					if={
						limit={
							ROOT={ 
								combat_rating >= 100
								has_focus = focus_hunting
							}
						}
						add_twenty_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_twenty_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					}
				}
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_terradon
					change_martial = 7
				}
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_stegadon
					change_martial = 8
				}
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_sauropod
					change_martial = 9
				}
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_thunder_lizard
					change_martial = 10
					add_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
				}
				10 = {
					give_nickname = nick_the_carnosaur
					change_martial = 15
					add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					if={
						limit={
							ROOT={ combat_rating >= 100 }
							NOT={ has_focus = focus_hunting }
						}
						add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_ten_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					}
					if={
						limit={
							ROOT={ 
								combat_rating >= 100
								has_focus = focus_hunting
							}
						}
						add_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_twenty_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_twenty_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_twenty_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
						add_twenty_five_duel_experience_modifier = yes
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = lustria.7
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if={limit={has_focus=focus_hunting}
			set_character_flag=the_rush_of_hunt
		}
	}
}
# Creature challenges us to combat
character_event = {
	id = lustria.7
	desc = lizardman207desc
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_dinosaur"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = duel }
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		save_event_target_as = combatant_1
		set_character_flag = flag_duel_no_draws
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = combatant_2
			set_character_flag = flag_duel_no_draws
			# Duel event
			character_event = {
				id = HFP.10095
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			# Kill off the creature to avoid shenanigans
			character_event = {
				id = lustria.8
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

# settlement_decision Choose whom you want to cut back your jungle
character_event = {
	id = lustria.10
	desc = lizardman261desc
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_jungle"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Do it yourself
	option = {
		name = lizardman261Adesc
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				in_command = no
				is_incapacitated_trigger = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_tribal = no
			}
			prestige = -50
		}
		else = {
			prestige = -25
		}
		random = { 
			chance = 5
			character_event={
				id = lustria.6
				days = 15
				random = 12
			}
			set_character_flag=the_rush_of_hunt
		}
		# Event to resolve cutting back for the liege doing it himself
		character_event = {
			id = lustria.11
			days = 20
			random = 30
		}
	}
	# Send the steward
	option = {
		name = lizardman261Bdesc
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				job_treasurer = {
					character = yes
					is_adult = yes
					in_command = no
					is_incapacitated_trigger = no
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			job_treasurer = {
				# Steward - Charged to cut back the Jungle
				letter_event = {
					id = lustria.15
				}
				random = { 
					chance = 2
					character_event={
						id = lustria.6
						days = 15
						random = 12
					}
					set_character_flag=the_rush_of_hunt
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_tribal = no
			}
			wealth = -50
		}
		else = {
			wealth = -25
		}
	}
	# Nevermind
	option = {
		name = lizardman261Cdesc
	}
}

						stewardship > 10
					}

					}

					}

								add_province_modifier = {

							location = { has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle }

						}
					}

						health > 3
					}

						health > 6

					}

					ROOT = {

						nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
					}
				}
				20 = {
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = has_tomb_rot
						nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
					}
				}
				20 = {

						nurgle_blessing_check_effect = yes
					}
				}
				20 = {

					}
				}
			}
		}

				}
			}
		}
	}

# on_five_year_pulse Spoils of the Lustrian jungle (lizardman only) grants random boon
character_event = {
	id = lustria.18
	hide_window = yes

	religion = old_ones

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		capital_scope = {
			location = { region = world_new_world_lustria }
		}
		any_demesne_province = {
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
				has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
				has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_demesne_province = {
				has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.50
			any_demesne_province = {
				has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			realm_stewardship > 25
		}
	}
	immediate={
		random_demesne_province={
			limit={
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
				}
				location = { region = world_new_world_lustria_central }
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_province_adventurer_skaven
			save_event_target_as = target_province
		}
		random_demesne_province={
			limit={
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
					has_province_modifier = lustria_oppressive_jungle
				}
				location = { 
					region = world_new_world_lustria_northern
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_province_adventurer
			save_event_target_as = target_province
		}
		
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		decadence = -10
		random_list = {
			# Holy plaques found
			40 = {
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.19
				}
			}
			# Wild beasts tamed
			20 = {
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.20
				}
			}
			# Valuable resources found
			20 = {
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.21
				}
			}
			10 = {
				trigger={event_target:target_province_adventurer_skaven={always=yes}}
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.19
				}
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.27
					days = 120
					random = 80
				}
			}
			10 = {
				trigger={event_target:target_province_adventurer={always=yes}}
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.19
				}
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.27
					days = 120
					random = 80
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = lustria.19
	desc = lizardman281desc
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_jungle"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = GodsBePraised
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_artifact = {
					has_artifact_flag = slann_gold
					count < 6
				}
			}
			add_artifact = slann_gold
		}
		else = {
			piety = 250
		}
	}
}

# on_siege_over_winner Religious Rebels seize a holding and destroy a building. Owner of the winning unit is ROOT. The taken Holding title is in FROM.
character_event = {
	id = lustria.24 #TOG.1065
	hide_window = yes

	religion_group = old_ones_group

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_character_flag = rampage_revolter
		rebel = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					location = {
						has_province_modifier = lustria_jungle
					}
				}
				destroy_random_building = yes
			}
			# The capital holding
			location = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							is_capital = yes
						}
						has_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_oppressive_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
					remove_province_modifier = lustria_dense_jungle
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							is_capital = yes
						}
						has_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_dense_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
					remove_province_modifier = lustria_medium_jungle
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							is_capital = yes
						}
						has_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = lustria_medium_jungle
						duration = -1
					}
					remove_province_modifier = lustria_light_jungle
				}
				holder_scope = {
					# Inform Holding owner
					character_event = {
						id = lustria.25
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# Inform Holding owner

# on_siege_over_loc_chars Rebels kill a local character. Siege winner unit owner in the 'new_character' scope, lost holding title in FROM, local character in ROOT.
character_event = {
	id = lustria.26 #TOG.1190
	desc = lizardman304desc
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war
	picture ="GFX_evt_lustria_dinosaur"

	religion_group = old_ones_group

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		new_character = {
			rebel = yes
			has_character_flag = rampage_revolter
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_female = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_adult = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		# Death
		new_character = {
			ROOT = {
				if = {
 					limit = { is_invincible_trigger = yes }
					antideath_effect = yes
					break = yes
				}
				death = {
					death_reason = death_rabble
					killer = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_TOG_1190
	}
}

		year > 2055
		is_doom_high_trigger = yes
		is_heretic = no

				grant_title = PREV

		}

	}

# on_decade_pulse A Skink Priest is generated from a spawning pool
character_event = {
	id = lustria.30
	title = slizardmen.1.title
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmens1
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_jungle

	religion = old_ones

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		higher_tier_than = COUNT
		NOT = {
			any_courtier = {
				trait = skink_priest
				count > 5
			}
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			any_province_holding = {
				OR = {
					has_building = ct_spawning_pool
					has_building = tp_spawning_pool
					has_building = ca_spawning_pool
				}
				count = 1
			}
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		factor = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			lower_tier_than = KING
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			higher_tier_than = KING
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						trait = lore_heavens
						trait = creature_skink
					}
					AND = {
						trait = lore_beasts
						trait = creature_skink
					}
				}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.20
			any_courtier = {
				trait = skink_priest
				count = 0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			any_courtier = {
				trait = skink_priest
				count > 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			any_courtier = {
				trait = skink_priest
				count > 3
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_realm_province = {
				any_province_holding = {
					ROOT = { is_liege_or_above = OWNER }
					OR = {
						has_building = ct_spawning_pool
						has_building = tp_spawning_pool
						has_building = ca_spawning_pool
					}
					count = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.50
			any_realm_province = {
				any_province_holding = {
					ROOT = { is_liege_or_above = OWNER }
					OR = {
						has_building = ct_spawning_pool
						has_building = tp_spawning_pool
						has_building = ca_spawning_pool
					}
					count = 3
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			any_realm_province = {
				any_province_holding = {
					ROOT = { is_liege_or_above = OWNER }
					OR = {
						has_building = ct_spawning_pool
						has_building = tp_spawning_pool
						has_building = ca_spawning_pool
					}
					count = 4
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			any_realm_province = {
				any_province_holding = {
					ROOT = { is_liege_or_above = OWNER }
					OR = {
						has_building = ct_spawning_pool
						has_building = tp_spawning_pool
						has_building = ca_spawning_pool
					}
					count > 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmens1
		piety = 50
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						attributes = { learning = 9 }
						dynasty = RANDOM
						religion = old_ones
						culture = lizardman
						female = no
						age = 16
					}
				}
				35 = {
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						attributes = { learning = 11 }
						dynasty = RANDOM
						religion = old_ones
						culture = lizardman
						female = no
						age = 16
					}
				}
				15 = {
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						attributes = { learning = 13 }
						dynasty = RANDOM
						religion = old_ones
						culture = lizardman
						female = no
						age = 16
					}
				}
				10 = {
					create_character = {
						random_traits = yes
						attributes = { learning = 15 }
						dynasty = RANDOM
						religion = old_ones
						culture = lizardman
						female = no
						age = 16
					}
				}
			}
			# Give Magic
			new_character = {
				piety = 20
				prestige = 50
				add_trait = creature_skink
				add_trait = skink_priest
				add_trait = zealous
				add_trait = bright
				set_character_flag = spawned_skink_priest
				random_list = {

		is_landed = yes
		higher_tier_than = BARON
	}

		capital_scope = {
			# Ping to province while the randomly selected heir is chosen automatically by Open Elective
			province_event = {
				id = lustria.32
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
# Ping to province while the randomly selected heir is chosen automatically by Open Elective

	id = lustria.32
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		holder_scope = {
			character_event = {
				id = lustria.33
			}
		}
	}
}
# Ping to elective event to choose inheritor
character_event = {
	id = lustria.33
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
							ROOT = {
								NOT = {
									any_courtier = {
										trait = creature_skink
										OR = {
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
										}
									}
								}
								NOT = {
									any_vassal = {
										trait = creature_skink
										OR = {
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					any_vassal = {
						has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
							ROOT = {
								NOT = {
									any_courtier = {
										trait = creature_skink
										OR = {
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
										}
									}
								}
								NOT = {
									any_vassal = {
										trait = creature_skink
										OR = {
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
											has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_vassal = {
				limit = {
					has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
				}
				# Lizardmen Inheritance Event
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.34
				}
				break = yes
			}
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
				}
				# Lizardmen Inheritance Event
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.34
				}
				break = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
						NOR = {
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						}
					}
					any_vassal = {
						has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
						NOR = {
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						}
					}
					NAND = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
						}
						any_vassal = {
							has_minor_title = title_skink_heir
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					any_vassal = {
						trait = creature_skink
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						}
					}
					any_courtier = {
						trait = creature_skink
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
							has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_vassal = {
				limit = {
					trait = creature_skink
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_3
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_4
					}
				}
				# Lizardmen Inheritance Event
				character_event = {
					id = lustria.34
				}
				break = yes
			}
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					trait = creature_skink
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_1
						has_character_modifier = magic_power_2

					}
				}

				character_event = {

		}
	}

# Lizardmen Inheritance Event
character_event = {
	id = lustria.34
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# if the elected party is of a band, destroy the title.
	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				mercenary = yes
			}
			activate_title = {
				title = THIS
				status = no
			}
			destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
		wealth = FROM
		FROM = {
			clear_wealth = THIS
			abdicate_to = ROOT
			any_claim = { remove_claim = PREV }
		}
		any_vassal = {
			remove_title = title_skink_heir
		}
		any_courtier = {
			remove_title = title_skink_heir
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			refill_holding_levy = yes
		}
		remove_title = title_skink_heir
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

# on_bi_yearly_pulse Get negative traits for not being contemplating enough, or remove them for being in deep slumber - Triggered by bi-yearly pulse
character_event = {
	id = lustria.35
	hide_window = yes

	religion = old_ones
	only_men = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = creature_slann
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
			}
			# Good event
			character_event = {
				id = lustria.36
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				# Good event
				60 = {
					character_event = {
						id = lustria.36
					}
				}
				# Bad event
				40 = {
					character_event = {
						id = lustria.37
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# Good event happens because of deep sleep
character_event = {
	id = lustria.36
	desc = lizardman103desc
	picture = "GFX_evt_lustria_slann"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = creature_slann
	}

	option = {
		name = lizardman103optA
		random_list = {
			# Lunacy
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = stressed
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = depressed
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = lunatic_3
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOR = {
						trait = stressed
						trait = depressed
						trait = lunatic_3
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						trait = stressed
						trait = depressed
						trait = lunatic_3
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "lunatic_counter"
						value = -15
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						trait = stressed
						trait = depressed
						NOT = { trait = lunatic_3 }
					}
					remove_trait = depressed
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						trait = stressed
						NOR = {
							trait = depressed
							trait = lunatic_3
						}
					}
					remove_trait = stressed
				}
				# Fallback
				else = {
					piety = -25
					prestige = -25
				}
			}
			# Healing
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { is_ill = yes }
				}
				healing_effect = yes
			}
			# Slothful
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { trait = slothful }
				}
				remove_trait = slothful
			}
			# Patience
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = patient
				}
				add_trait = patient
			}
			# Diligence
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = diligent
				}
				add_trait = diligent
			}
			# General boost
			25 = {
				piety = 50
				prestige = 50
			}
		}
	}
}
# Bad event happens because of being awake
character_event = {
	id = lustria.37
	desc = lizardman102desc
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = creature_slann
	}

	option = {
		name = lizardman102optA
		random_list = {
			# Lunacy
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					NOT = { trait = stressed }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					NOT = { trait = depressed }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					NOT = { trait = lunatic_3 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = lunatic_3
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						trait = stressed
						trait = depressed
						NOT = { trait = lunatic_3 }
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = "lunatic_counter"
						value = 5
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						# lunacy Ping
						character_event = { id = mutate.5 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						trait = stressed
						NOR = {
							trait = depressed
							trait = lunatic_3
						}
					}
					add_trait = depressed
				}
				else = {
					add_trait = stressed
				}
			}
			# Illness
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_ill = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dlc = "Reapers"
						}
					}
					add_trait = ill
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_dlc = "Reapers"
					}
					add_symptom_effect = yes
				}
			}
			# Slothful
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					trait = slothful
				}
				add_trait = slothful
			}
			# Patience
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { trait = patient }
				}
				remove_trait = patient
			}
			# Diligence
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
				}
				remove_trait = diligent
			}
			# General malus
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOR = {
						piety > 50
						prestige > 50
					}
				}
				piety = -50
				prestige = -50
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = lustria.43
	title = EVTNAMEslizardmen8
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen8

	religion_group = old_ones_group
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = {
		has_job_action = action_explore_ruins
		NOT = { trait = maimed }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { martial = 2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { martial = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { martial = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { martial = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			martial = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			martial = 11
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			martial = 12
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			martial = 13
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				# Wounded
				75 = {
					set_character_flag = chancellor_wounded
				}
				# Maimed
				25 = {
					set_character_flag = chancellor_maimed
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVOPTAslizardmen8
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = chancellor_wounded
		}
		add_trait = wounded
		clr_character_flag = chancellor_wounded
		liege = {
			# Liege gets a letter about Chancellor being wounded
			letter_event = {
				id = slizardmen.9
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVOPTBslizardmen8
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = chancellor_maimed
		}
		add_trait = maimed
		liege = {
			letter_event = { id = slizardmen.10 }
		}
		clr_character_flag = chancellor_maimed
	}
}

#The Lizardmen scourges enemy province to take sacrifical prisoners
# ROOT is attacker, FROM is province sieged
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.13
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen13
	picture = GFX_evt_lizardmen_saurus
	religion_group = old_ones_group

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		religion_group = old_ones_group
		FROM = { NOT = { location = { has_province_modifier = province_slave_raid } } }
		FROM = { NOT = { location = { has_province_modifier = province_scourged } } }
		FROM = { NOT = { location = { has_province_modifier = province_slave_raid_chaos_dwarf } } }
		any_war = { attacker = { character = ROOT }
				using_cb = flower_war_raid }
		FROM = { is_capital = yes
			NOT = { culture = nehekharan }
			owner = {
				NOR = {
					trait = creature_nehekharan
					is_vampire_visible_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		} #only against the living
	}

	option = { #Take all and burn their lands!
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen13
		if = { limit = { FROM = { owner = { top_liege = { NOT = { character = PREV } } } } }
			FROM = { owner = { top_liege = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.15 } } } }
			}
		FROM = { owner = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.14 } } }
		FROM = { set_province_flag = flag_province_scourged }
		if = { limit = { FROM = { OR = { any_neighbor_province = { is_tribal = yes }
						has_province_flag = flag_province_scourged
						NOT = { num_of_settlements = 2 }
						}
						NOT = { is_nomadic = yes }
					}
				}
			random = { chance = 1
			FROM = { convert_to = TRIBAL }
				} #closesrandom
			} #closesif
		if = { limit = { FROM = { location = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = province_scourged } } } }
			FROM = { location = { add_province_modifier = { name = province_scourged
						duration = 900 } }
				}
		 } #closesif

		wealth = 150
		prestige = 150
		piety = 250
		decadence = 1
		change_variable = { which = "sacrifical_victims" value = 2 }
		if = { limit = { ai = yes }
		change_variable = { which = "sacrifical_victims" value = 2 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				ROOT = { OR = { trait = lunatic_3
						trait = lunatic_2 } }
				}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = cruel
				}
			}
	}
	option = { #Just take them all!
		name = EVTOPTCslizardmen13
		if = { limit = { FROM = { owner = { top_liege = { NOT = { character = PREV } } } } }
			FROM = { owner = { top_liege = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.16 } } } }
			}
		if = { limit = { FROM = { location = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = province_slave_raid } } } }
			FROM = { location = { add_province_modifier = { name = province_slave_raid
									duration = 1000 } }
				}
		 } #closesif
		FROM = { owner = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.16 } } }
		wealth = 25
		prestige = 10
		piety = 10
		change_variable = { which = "sacrifical_victims" value = 6 }
		if = { limit = { ai = yes }
		change_variable = { which = "sacrifical_victims" value = 5 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ROOT = { NOR = { trait = possessed
						trait = lunatic_3
						trait = lunatic_2 } }
				}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.7
				trait = zealous
				}
			}
	}
	option = { #I don't care about this province
		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen13
		piety = -25
		prestige = -25
		if = { limit = { trait = cruel }
			random = { chance = 1
				remove_trait = cruel }
			}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				ROOT = { NOR = { trait = possessed
						trait = lunatic_3
						trait = lunatic_2 } }
				}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = kind
				}
			}
	}
}

	option = {

	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen22006
	picture = GFX_evt_lizardmen_saurus

	only_men = yes
	min_age = 14
	max_age = 350
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_rulers = yes
	religion = old_ones

	trigger = {
		uses_decadence = yes
		trait = honest
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 150
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen22006
		decadence = -1
	}
}

############################

####The Sleeping Slann#########

# Umbrella event
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.23
	hide_window = yes

	only_men = yes
	min_age = 2000
	religion = old_ones
	ai = yes

	trigger = {
		trait = creature_slann
		trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
		independent = no
		top_liege = {
			culture_group = lizardman_group
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 6
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				top_liege = {
					character_event = { id = slizardmen.24 }
				}
			}
			# Reclined his head on a different side
			39 = {
				top_liege = {
					character_event = { id = slizardmen.25 }
				}
			}	# Flies around his body
			20 = {
				top_liege = {
					character_event = { id = slizardmen.26 }
				}
			}	# Snores
			1 = {
				top_liege = {
					character_event = { id = slizardmen.27 }
				}
			}	# Asks for maggot soup
		}
	}
}

# A Skink agrees with your evaluation of the Slann's command
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.23001
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen23001
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes
	notification = yes

	immediate = { decadence = -1
			if = { limit = { FROM = { trait = skink_priest } }
				decadence = -7 }
			if = { limit = { FROM = { is_ruler = yes } }
				decadence = -4 }
			if = { limit = { FROM = { trait = defective } }
				decadence = 1 }
			}
	option = {
		}
}

# A Skink disagrees with your evaluation of the Slann's command
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.23002
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen23002
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes
	notification = yes

	immediate = { decadence = 4
			if = { limit = { FROM = { trait = skink_priest } }
				decadence = 10 }
			if = { limit = { FROM = { is_ruler = yes } }
				decadence = 5 }
			if = { limit = { FROM = { trait = defective } }
				decadence = -3 }
			}
	option = {
		}
}

# The Slann reclined his head in a different position
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.24
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen24
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		not = {
			trait = creature_slann
		}
	}

	option = { #He wants a ritual to be performed!
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen24
		piety = 50
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					trait = creature_skink
					is_ruler = yes
				}
				character_event = { id = slizardmen.24001 }
			}
			any_courtier = {
				limit = {
					trait = skink_priest
					NOT = {
						is_ruler = yes
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = slizardmen.24001 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #He's warning us of a coming threat!
		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen24
		prestige = 50
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.24002 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = skink_priest
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.24002 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #He's wants to be moved to a better position!
		name = EVTOPTCslizardmen24
		piety = 25
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.24003 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.24003 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #He's wants his neck to be cleaned!
		name = EVTOPTDslizardmen24
		prestige = 25
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.24004 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = skink_priest
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.24004 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}
}

# The Skink Hierophant believes the Slann wants a ritual to be performed
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.24001
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen24001
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	# I Agree
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen24001
		FROM = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.23001 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 45
			modifier = { factor = 1.5
				trait = zealous
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.5
				trait = diligent
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.5
				trait = cynical
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.75
				trait = slothful
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = brave }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = mystic }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = diligent }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = zealous }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = ambitious }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.85
				FROMFROM = { trait = cynical }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.85
				FROMFROM = { trait = slothful }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.85
				FROMFROM = { trait = gluttonous }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.85
				FROMFROM = { trait = craven }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.85
				FROMFROM = { trait = content }
				}
		 }
	}
	option = {	# I disagree
		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen24001
		FROM = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.23002 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 55
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM
						 value = 20 } }
				}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM
						 value = 0 } }
				}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.75
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM
						 value = -50 } }
				}

		}
	}
}

# Flies are flying in strange shape around the Slann's head
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.25
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen25
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		not = {
			trait = creature_slann
		}
	}
	option = { #They're mimicking a costellation to look for!
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen25
		piety = 50
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25001 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = skink_priest
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25001 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #They're showing the flow of magic!
		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen25
		prestige = 50
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25002 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = skink_priest
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25002 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #He called them to use as component for some spell!
		name = EVTOPTCslizardmen25
		piety = 25
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25003 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25003 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #They're sucking his sweat! Shoo them!
		name = EVTOPTDslizardmen25
		prestige = 25
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25004 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = skink_priest
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.25004 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.25002
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen25002
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	# I Agree
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen25002
		FROM = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.23001 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 55
			modifier = { factor = 1.5
				trait = paranoid
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.5
				trait = mystic
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.5
				trait = trusting
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.75
				trait = hunter
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.75
				FROM = { trait = skink_priest }
				NOT = { trait = skink_priest }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 0.35
				FROM = { NOT = { trait = skink_priest } }
				trait = skink_priest
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = diligent }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25
				FROMFROM = { trait = scholar }
				}
			modifier = { factor = 1.25

		}
	}

		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen26
		piety = 50

							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.26001 } }
				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = skink_priest
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.26001 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #He's casting a very complicate spell!
		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen26

							is_ruler = yes }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.26002 } }

							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }
						character_event = { id = slizardmen.26002 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}

	option = { #The light is bothering him!

		piety = 25
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							is_ruler = yes }

				any_courtier = { limit = { trait = creature_skink
							NOT = { is_ruler = yes } }

# LIZARDMEN GREAT EXPEDITION

character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.28
	hide_window = yes

	only_men = yes
	min_age = 2000
	religion = old_ones
	ai = yes

	trigger = {
			religion_authority = 0.05
		NOT = { creature_slann = { has_character_modifier = tablet_cooldown } }
		any_independent_ruler = { NOT = { religion_group = old_ones_group }
					higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
		independent = no

		}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 83
	}

	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = tablet_cooldown
			hidden = yes
			duration = 10950
		}
		top_liege = { long_character_event = { id = slizardmen.29 } }
	}
}

# The Slann calls for a great mission.
long_character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.29
	title = EVTTITLEslizardmen29
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen29
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen29
		piety = 50
		spawn_fleet = {
			province = closest
			owner = ROOT
			match_character = ROOT
			match_mult = 2
			match_min = 100
			disband_on_peace = yes
			earmark = liz_fleet
		}
		set_character_flag = sanctioned_by_slann
			random_independent_ruler = { limit = { NOT = { religion_group = old_ones_group }
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { capital_scope = { region = world_dragon_isles } }
										is_landed = yes
										is_nomadic = no
										any_demesne_title = { tier = KING }
										higher_tier_than = DUKE }
						hidden_tooltip = { long_character_event = { id = slizardmen.29001 } }

						random_realm_province = {
									ROOT = {
										war = {
											casus_belli = tablet_search
											target = PREVPREVPREV # The top liege of the owner
											thirdparty_title = PREVPREV # The de jure kingdom
											tier = KING
											}
										}
									}
								 }

		hidden_tooltip = { any_independent_ruler = { limit = { religion = ROOT
								capital_scope = { region = world_new_world }
								NOT = { character = ROOT } }
								long_character_event = { id = slizardmen.29002 days = 2 random = 7 } } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

##################################
###THE SLANN AWAKENING EVENTS#####

#On each declared war (on_action), check if there's a Slann vassal and see if he awakes or frowns on the war.
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.30
	hide_window = yes

	only_independent=yes
	religion_group=old_ones_group
	culture_group=lizardman_group
	trigger = {
		any_vassal = {
			trait = creature_slann
			trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
		}
		trait = creature_skink
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { FROM = { trait = creature_skink } }
			FROM = {
				random_list = {
					95 = {
						modifier = { factor = 0.85
							trait = ambitious
						}
						modifier = { factor = 0.85
							trait = diligent
						}
						modifier = { factor = 1.25
							trait = slothful }
					}
					4 = { #Restless Slann, abort the war?
						random_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_slann }
								character_event = { id = slizardmen.31 days = 100 random = 50 }
						}
						modifier = { factor = 0 any_war = { using_cb = tablet_search } }
					}
					1 = { #Slann awakens to fight
						random_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_slann }
							character_event = { id = slizardmen.32 days = 7 random = 7 }
						}
						modifier = { factor = 10 any_war = { using_cb = tablet_search } }
					}
			 	}
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { ROOT = { trait = creature_skink } }
			ROOT = {
				random_list = {
					95 = {
						modifier = { factor = 0.85 trait = ambitious }
						modifier = { factor = 0.85 trait = diligent }
						modifier = { factor = 1.25 trait = slothful }
					}
					4 = { #Restless Slann, abort the war?
						random_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_slann }
							character_event = { id = slizardmen.31 days = 100 random = 50 }
						}
						modifier = { factor = 0 any_war = { using_cb = tablet_search } }
					}
					1 = { #Slann awakens to fight
						random_vassal = { limit = { trait = creature_slann }
							character_event = { id = slizardmen.32 days = 7 random = 7 }
						}
						modifier = { factor = 10 any_war = { using_cb = tablet_search } }
					}
			 	}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Slann has awaken, step aside
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.32005
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen32005
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { war = yes
			NOT = { has_character_flag = warring_slann } }

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen32005
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_trait = s_target_trait
			add_friend = FROM	#To keep track
			FROM = {
				remove_trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
				set_character_flag = warring_slann
				save_event_target_as = awakened_slaan
				wealth = ROOT
				ROOT = { clear_wealth = THIS }
				any_demesne_title = { set_title_flag = old_slann_demesne }
				ROOT = {
					abdicate_to = FROM
					any_claim = { remove_claim = PREV }
					character_event = { id = slizardmen.32006 days = 1}
				}
				set_government_type = lizardmen_government_1
			}
		}

	}
}

#On war ended (on action) the Slann goes to rest again.
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.33
	hide_window = yes

	only_rulers = yes
	religion_group=old_ones_group

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			FROM = { has_character_flag = warring_slann }
			ROOT = { has_character_flag = warring_slann }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = warring_slann } }
			ROOT = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.33005 days = 2 random = 4 } }
		}
		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_character_flag = warring_slann } }
			FROM = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.33005 days = 2 random = 4 } }
		}
	}
}

# The Slann returns to sleep and gives the titles back to the Skink
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.33005
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen33005
	picture = GFX_evt_lustria_slann

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen33005
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = { limit = { s_target_trait = { any_friend = { character = ROOT } } }
				s_target_trait = { limit = { any_friend = { character = ROOT } }
					wealth = ROOT
					ROOT = { clear_wealth = THIS }
					ROOT = { abdicate_to = PREV }
					any_demesne_title = { limit = { has_title_flag = old_slann_demesne }
								grant_title = ROOT
								clr_title_flag = old_slann_demesne }
					set_government_type = lizardmen_government
					remove_trait = s_target_trait
					remove_friend = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {  clr_character_flag = warring_slann
						any_claim = { remove_claim = PREV }
						set_government_type = theocracy_government
						add_trait = lizardman_sleepingslann }
				break = yes
			}

			if = { limit = { NOT = { s_target_trait = { any_friend = { character = ROOT } } } }
				random_courtier = { limit = { trait = creature_skink }
					wealth = ROOT
					ROOT = { clear_wealth = THIS }
					ROOT = { abdicate_to = PREV }
					any_demesne_title = { limit = { has_title_flag = old_slann_demesne }
						grant_title = ROOT
						clr_title_flag = old_slann_demesne
					}
					set_government_type = lizardmen_government
					remove_trait = s_target_trait
					remove_opinion = { who=ROOT modifier=opinion_formerskink_beacon }
				}
				ROOT = {  clr_character_flag = warring_slann
					any_claim = { remove_claim = PREV }
					set_government_type = theocracy_government
					add_trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
				}
				break = yes
			}
			if = { limit = { NOT = { s_target_trait = { any_friend = { character = ROOT } } }
				NOT = { any_courtier = { trait = creature_skink } }
				}
				create_random_steward = {
					random_traits = yes
					dynasty = random
					culture = ROOT
					religion = ROOT
					female = no
				}
				new_character = {
					add_trait = creature_skink
					wealth = ROOT
					ROOT = { clear_wealth = THIS }
					ROOT = { abdicate_to = PREV }
					any_demesne_title = { limit = { has_title_flag = old_slann_demesne }
						grant_title = ROOT
						clr_title_flag = old_slann_demesne
					}
					set_government_type = lizardmen_government
					remove_trait = s_target_trait
					remove_opinion = { who=ROOT modifier=opinion_formerskink_beacon }
				}
				ROOT = {  clr_character_flag = warring_slann
					any_claim = { remove_claim = PREV }
					set_government_type = theocracy_government
					add_trait = lizardman_sleepingslann
				}
				break = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

					modifier = { factor=0.85 trait=ambitious }

								defender = {
									character = ROOT
									NOT = { war_score = 0 }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = { factor=0.75

							any_war = {

####Investigate Alignment Plot events
# A plot backer sees an opportunity - The Skink is a drunkard
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.35
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen35
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	religion_group = old_ones_group

	trigger = {
		plot_target_char = { trait = drunkard }
		any_backed_character = {
			has_plot = plot_investigate_alignment
			plot_power = 0.5
			plot_target_char = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				trait = creature_skink
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			}
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = {
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 541

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
			has_plot = plot_investigate_alignment
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = {
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.10
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {

# A plot backer sees an opportunity - The Skink is an addict
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.36
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen36
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = old_ones_group
	is_part_of_plot = yes
	trigger = {
		plot_target_char = { trait = addict }
		any_backed_character = {
			has_plot = plot_investigate_alignment
			plot_power = 0.5
			plot_target_char = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				trait = creature_skink
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			}
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = {
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}

		}
	}

	only_men = yes

	max_age = 350
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_rulers = yes
	religion = old_ones
	ai = no

	option = { #Take noses
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen43
		piety = 150
	}

		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen43
		prestige = 300
		decadence = 1
	}

		name = EVTOPTCslizardmen43

		decadence = 1
	}
}

# The captured Amazon
long_character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.44
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen44
	picture = "GFX_evt_amazon_queen"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 350
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_playable = yes
	religion = old_ones
	ai = no

	option = { #Take tech inside her
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen44
		trigger = { OR = { trait = skink_priest
				trait = creature_slann } }
		military_techpoints = 75
		piety = 50
	}
	option = { #Take as pet for zoo
		name = EVTOPTBslizardmen44
		create_character = {
			random_traits = yes
			dynasty = random
			religion = amazon
			culture = amazon_main
			female = yes
			age = 23
			attributes = { martial = 15}
			trait = creature_amazon
			trait = brave
		}
		new_character = { imprison=ROOT add_rival=ROOT }
		prestige = 300
		piety = 150
		decadence = 2
	}
	option = { #Steal her stuff
		name = EVTOPTCslizardmen44
		wealth = 50
		decadence = 1
	}
}

# You're complacent! And therefore banished!
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.44101
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen44101
	picture = "GFX_evt_amazon"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen44101
		remove_trait = complacent
		add_trait = questing
		remove_trait = creature_amazon
		add_trait = creature_human
		add_trait = disinherited_amazon
		banish = yes
		random_list  = {
			35 = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.44001 days = 900 random = 900 } } #Died honorably
			35 = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.44003 days = 900 random = 900 } } #Died dishonorably
			25 = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.44005 days = 900 random = 900 } } #Became submissive
			5 = {
				modifier = { factor = 1.4
						trait = brave }
				modifier = { factor = 1.4
						trait = strong }
				modifier = { factor = 1.4
						trait = wroth }
				modifier = { factor = 1.4
						trait = hunter }
				modifier = { factor = 1.4
						trait = duelist }
				modifier = { factor = 1.4
						trait = brilliant_strategist }
				modifier = { factor = 0.4
						trait = craven }
				character_event = { id = slizardmen.44007 days = 900 random = 900 }
			} #Returns in glory
		}
	}
}

#Died honorably
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.44001
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen44001
	picture = "GFX_evt_amazon"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen44001
		if = { limit = { is_invincible_trigger = yes }
			antideath_effect = yes
			break = yes
		}
		death = { death_reason = death_battle }
		FROMFROMFROM = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.44002 } }
	}
}

# Became tamed
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.44005
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen44005
	picture = "GFX_evt_amazon"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen44005
		remove_trait = questing
		any_independent_ruler = { limit = { religion_group = old_world_group }
			ROOT = { move_character = PREV
				remove_trait = creature_amazon
				add_trait = creature_human
				culture = PREV
				religion = PREV

				remove_trait = brave
				remove_trait = wroth
				remove_trait = cruel
				add_trait = content
				random = {
					chance=25
					add_trait=gluttonous
					add_trait = is_fat
				}
				random = { chance=25 add_trait = kind }
				random = { chance=25 add_trait=drunkard }
				random = { chance=25 add_trait=addict }
			}
		}
		FROMFROMFROM = { character_event = { id = slizardmen.44006 } }
	}
}

####Faction to remove Complacent Amazon
# Amazon Queen receives ultimatum letter
letter_event = {
	id = slizardmen.45
	desc = EVTDESCslizardmen45

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_complacent_queen }
	}

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_complacent_queen
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen45
		ai_chance = {

	}

					trait = scholarly_theologian
					trait = mastermind_theologian } }
		hidden_tooltip = { long_character_event = { id = slizardmen.78 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}

			decadence = 20 }
		hidden_tooltip = { long_character_event = { id = slizardmen.79 } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1
				modifier = { factor = 0
					trait = creature_skink }
			 }
	}
}

#Fire for the Player, check if courtier Amazons available
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.82
	hide_window = yes

	only_women = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 350
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	only_rulers = yes
	religion = amazon
	ai = no

	trigger = { war = no
		 trait = creature_amazon
		NOR = { trait = complacent
			trait = questing
			trait = pregnant
			trait = hard_pregnancy

#Drunkard
character_event = {
	id = slizardmen.83
	desc = { text = EVTDESCAslizardmen83
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = gregarious } } }
	desc = { text = EVTDESCBslizardmen83
		trigger = { trait = gregarious } }

	picture = GFX_evt_slaanesh_tempt

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAslizardmen83
		decadence = 3
		if = { limit = { NOT = { trait = gregarious } }
			random = { chance = 60
				add_trait = drunkard
				decadence = 8 }
			 }
		if = { limit = { trait = gregarious }
			random = { chance = 40
				add_trait = drunkard
				decadence = 3 }
			 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}
